               <h1 class="post-title entry-title">
                What is Malware? Malicious Software
               </h1>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="author2">
                 <b>
                  By:
                 </b>
                 <a href="https://plus.google.com/100459174466438792296">
                  Melvin Corney
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_date">

               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <span id="8447789096704342174">
                 <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   What is Malware?
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  Malware is short for Malicious Software, which is any software intended to and or designed to harm your computer.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   Examples of Malware?
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  Some examples of malware can included Viruses, Worms, Spyware, Ransomware, Rootkits, Keyloggers, and Adware.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   The Purpose of Malware?
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  The purpose of malware is to infect, harm, and or collect data from your computer. The data it collects can be anything from personal Login Information to Social Security and Bank Account Numbers.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   Who Creates Malware?
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  Software Developers with malicious intent.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eUhu2OV4aA0/UrkdKhl_POI/AAAAAAAAGIg/sAaUMz31YQY/s1600/Malicious-Software-Malware.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img alt="Malware Malicious Software MalwareBytes" border="0" height="300" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eUhu2OV4aA0/UrkdKhl_POI/AAAAAAAAGIg/sAaUMz31YQY/s1600/Malicious-Software-Malware.jpg" title="What is Malware?" width="400"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   How can Malware infect my computer?
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  Their are numerous ways that malware can infect your computer below are listed some scenarios.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   From the Internet:
                  </b>
                  Most Malware is distributed through the internet, Why? because it spreads quickly and anyone can make and upload it.
                  <b>
                   Email:
                  </b>
                  This can be through emails services such as Outlook, Gmail, Yahoo, and other email services. Watch for suspicious emails asking you to confirm your account number and social security information, in some cases even asking you to accept money.
                  <b>
                   Websites:
                  </b>
                  The most dangerous are Pornography, Social, Gambling, Survey, P2P, and Gaming websites.
                  <b>
                   Downloads:
                  </b>
                  When you download software online from unknown publishers.
                  <b>
                   Pop-up Window:
                  </b>
                  When you browse some websites you may encounter a pop-up window that insists that you download and install their software (This is known as a scare tactic). It may look as if it is scanning your system. You can use (Ctrl-Alt-Delete) to access Task Manager to end the pop-up window.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   From Friends and Family:
                  </b>
                  Believe it or not you can catch a virus as quickly as anyone else connected to the internet.
                  <b>
                   Media:
                  </b>
                  Such as a USB Flash Drive, CD or DVDs which contains documents may sometimes contain unwanted software which may infect your computer unless you have Antivirus Software installed on your system.
                  <b>
                   Email:
                  </b>
                  As we mentioned above.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   Software:
                  </b>
                  Some software you install can include Adware. Adware is a program that is designed to automatically download and display advertisement. The advertisement is used to generate income for its author. You have Adware if you experience random redirects to websites you don't remember clicking and popups.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <a href="http://www.hypersmash.com/">
                   Hypersmash.com
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   Pirated Software:
                  </b>
                  If you download pirated software beware you can easily be downloading malware as well. It may look legitimate but in most cases its just a scam.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Malware can be designed to take full control of your computer we highly recommended that you scan your computer for Malware even if your computer doesn't have any of the symptoms above.
                 </div>
                </span>
